function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 77') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.77!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_country')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_country');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_country')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_country');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_country') != '77690b3ab42a17e00a18ade6fa1692801df106db') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_country');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_country', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_country');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_country') !== '77690b3ab42a17e00a18ade6fa1692801df106db') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_country') !== '6124ffad5b47f50069247361aecfc5aeca19ce9f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_country');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_country');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_country')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_country', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_country') !== '77690b3ab42a17e00a18ade6fa1692801df106db') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_country');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php') != 'df38c5e287ee2ecc9e910dbff0e96f00514c8c98') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php') !== 'df38c5e287ee2ecc9e910dbff0e96f00514c8c98') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php') !== '8cdd4a2a7c2e94d5e4268d06e5789394e775e75d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php') !== 'df38c5e287ee2ecc9e910dbff0e96f00514c8c98') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/system/000_registration/registration.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/setup.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup.js');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup.js') != 'e9a7b69ed767c40df9d2652551c0b3e460f922e0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== 'e9a7b69ed767c40df9d2652551c0b3e460f922e0') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== '2b978000a0c36f26f0ec6426e24de6f3e94c6c05') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== 'e9a7b69ed767c40df9d2652551c0b3e460f922e0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') != '94881e49fdb2110826329a68ee3263934a6c3309') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') !== '94881e49fdb2110826329a68ee3263934a6c3309') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') !== 'e44f1594939e9e1f1ed3f472fba6c98702911c19') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql') !== '94881e49fdb2110826329a68ee3263934a6c3309') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country.sql');
		}
	}
}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/struct_with_examples.sql.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/struct_with_examples.sql.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/struct_with_examples.sql.php') !== '1ecce3261ea2ddae555f8f7440b5590ba3a23d7e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/struct_with_examples.sql.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 78\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 78') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
